country_event = {
	id = twrgermanengland.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrgermanengland.2"}
		title = twrgermanengland.2.t
		desc = twrgermanengland.2.d
		picture = GFX_report_event_business_as_usual

		is_triggered_only = yes
		fire_only_once = yes

		option = {
			name = twrgermanengland.2.a
			ai_chance = { 
				factor = 50
			}
			add_stability = 0.01
			hidden_effect = { GER = { country_event = { days = 0 id = twrgermany.30 } } }
		}

		option = {
			name = twrgermanengland.2.b
			ai_chance = { 
				factor = 0
			}
			add_political_power = -100
			add_stability = -0.5
			hidden_effect = {
				hidden_effect = { GER = { country_event = { days = 0 id = twrgermany.31 } } }
			}
			add_named_threat = { 
				threat = 10
				name = ENG_shot_them_down
			}
		}
	}

	country_event = {
	id = twrgermanengland.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrgermanengland.3"}
		title = twrgermanengland.3.t
		desc = twrgermanengland.3.d
		picture = GFX_report_event_business_as_usual

		is_triggered_only = yes

		fire_only_once = yes

		option = {
			name = twrgermanengland.3.a
			ai_chance = { 
				factor = 50
			}
			add_stability = 0.01
			hidden_effect = {
				set_global_flag = brits_avoided_a_war
			}
		}

		option = {
			name = twrgermanengland.3.b
			ai_chance = { 
				factor = 0
			}
			add_political_power = -100
			add_stability = -0.5
			hidden_effect = {
				set_global_flag = shoot_them_down
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = GER
				type = topple_government
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Election Results - labour wins
	id = twrbritainpolitics.999
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainpolitics.999"}
	title = twrbritainpolitics.999.t
	desc = twrbritainpolitics.999.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_election

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.999.a
		news_event = { days = 1 id = twrnews.18 }
		complete_national_focus = ENG_attlee_labour
		custom_effect_tooltip = LABOUR_DECISIONS_OPENED_TT
		set_country_flag = LABOUR_WINS_FIRST_ELECTION
		#
		# the parliament mechanic stuff
		set_temp_variable =  { temp_party = 1 }
		ENG_house_of_commons_change_to_government = yes
		set_temp_variable =  { temp_party = 2 }
		ENG_house_of_commons_change_to_opposition = yes
		set_temp_variable =  { temp_party = 3 }
		ENG_house_of_commons_change_to_opposition = yes
		#
	}
}

country_event = { #Election Results - cons win
	id = twrbritainpolitics.998
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainpolitics.998"}
	title = twrbritainpolitics.998.t
	desc = twrbritainpolitics.998.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_election

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.998.a
		news_event = { days = 1 id = twrnews.19 }
		complete_national_focus = ENG_butler_conservative
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = conservative
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = conservative
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		set_temp_variable =  { temp_party = 3 }
		ENG_house_of_commons_change_to_government = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = CONSERVATIVE_DECISIONS_OPENED_TT
		set_country_flag = CON_MINISTERS_ALLOWED
		clr_country_flag = LAB_MINISTERS_ALLOWED
		set_country_flag = CONS_WIN_FIRST_ELECTION

		add_ideas = ENG_HoG_Peter_Thorneycroft
		add_ideas = ENG_AM_Edward_Heath
		add_ideas = ENG_MoS_David_Maxwell_Fyfe
		add_ideas = ENG_PA_Alec_DouglasHome
		#
		# the parliament mechanic stuff
		set_temp_variable =  { temp_party = 1 }
		ENG_house_of_commons_change_to_opposition = yes
		set_temp_variable =  { temp_party = 2 }
		ENG_house_of_commons_change_to_opposition = yes
		set_temp_variable =  { temp_party = 3 }
		ENG_house_of_commons_change_to_government = yes
		#

	}
}

country_event = { #Election Results - hung parliament
	id = twrbritainpolitics.997
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainpolitics.997"}
	title = twrbritainpolitics.997.t
	desc = twrbritainpolitics.997.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_election

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.997.a
		set_country_flag = UK_hung_parliament_1
		news_event = { days = 1 id = twrnews.21 }
		complete_national_focus = ENG_hung_parliament
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_COALITION_NEGOTIATIONS
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					ENG = {
						check_variable = {
			                var = 3.house_of_commons_seats
			                value = 1.house_of_commons_seats
			                compare = greater_than_or_equals
			            }
					}
				}
				country_event = { days = 10 id = twrbritainpolitics.362 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { days = 5 id = twrbritainpolitics.361 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #2nd Election begins - CONSERVATIVE PERSPECTIVE
	id = twrbritainpolitics.400
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainpolitics.400"}
	title = twrbritainpolitics.400.t
	desc = twrbritainpolitics.400.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_election

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.400.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_new_election_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_playing_as_conservatives
		hidden_effect = {
			# total of 31 days #
			country_event = { days = 4 id = twrbritainpolitics.401 }
			country_event = { days = 7 id = twrbritainpolitics.402 } # labour attacks our record
			country_event = { days = 9 id = twrbritainpolitics.4065 } # labour make gains
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_completed_focus = ENG_mr_butlers_mandate # butler survives
				}
				country_event = { days = 12 id = twrbritainpolitics.404 } # butler criticised for his weakness
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					has_completed_focus = ENG_magic_circles_grasp # butler got removed
				}
				country_event = { days = 12 id = twrbritainpolitics.405 } # thorneycroft attacked for his youth
			}
			country_event = { days = 15 id = twrbritainpolitics.4066 } # labour make gains
			country_event = { days = 19 id = twrbritainpolitics.406 } # minor MP scandal
			country_event = { days = 26 id = twrbritainpolitics.407 } # late stage labour campaigning
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Labour launch their campaign
	id = twrbritainpolitics.401
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainpolitics.401"}
	title = twrbritainpolitics.401.t
	desc = twrbritainpolitics.401.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.401.a
		add_political_power = 20
		add_to_variable = {
			var = ENG_labour_gain
			value = 10
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = ENG_labour_poll
			value = 10
			tooltip = LAB_gain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = ENG_conservative_gain
				value = 10
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = ENG_conservative_poll
				value = 10
			}
			set_country_flag = ENG_labour_launches_campaign_2nd_election
		}
	}
}


country_event = { # Labour attacks our record - (accuses us of being for the rich)
	id = twrbritainpolitics.402
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainpolitics.402"}
	title = twrbritainpolitics.402.t
	desc = twrbritainpolitics.402.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # downplay it
		name = twrbritainpolitics.402.a
		add_political_power = 10
		add_to_variable = {
			var = ENG_labour_gain
			value = 5
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = ENG_labour_poll
			value = 5
			tooltip = LAB_gain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = ENG_conservative_gain
				value = 5
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = ENG_conservative_poll
				value = 5
			}
			set_country_flag = ENG_labour_attacks_con_economic_policy
		}
	}
	option = { # hit back
		name = twrbritainpolitics.402.b
		add_political_power = -25
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ENG_labour_attacks_con_economic_policy
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
        		country_event = { days = 1 id = twrbritainpolitics.4021 }
    		}
    		50 = {
        		country_event = { days = 1 id = twrbritainpolitics.4022 }
    		}
    	}
	}
}

country_event = { # Minor MP scandal

	desc = twrbritainpolitics.406.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # accept it
		name = twrbritainpolitics.406.a
		add_political_power = 10
		add_to_variable = {
			var = ENG_labour_gain
			value = 3
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = ENG_labour_poll
			value = 3
			tooltip = LAB_gain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = ENG_conservative_gain
				value = 3
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = ENG_conservative_poll
				value = 3
			}
			set_country_flag = ENG_con_MP_scandal
		}
	}
	option = { # try to cover it up
		name = twrbritainpolitics.406.b
		add_political_power = -35
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ENG_con_MP_scandal
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
        		country_event = { days = 2 id = twrbritainpolitics.4041 }
    		}
    		50 = {
        		country_event = { days = 2 id = twrbritainpolitics.4042 }
    		}
    	}
	}
}

country_event = { #2nd Election begins - LABOUR PERSPECTIVE
	id = twrbritainpolitics.450
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainpolitics.450"}
	title = twrbritainpolitics.450.t
	desc = twrbritainpolitics.450.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_election

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.450.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_new_election_tt
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_playing_as_labour
		hidden_effect = {
			# total of 31 days #
			country_event = { days = 4 id = twrbritainpolitics.451 }
			country_event = { days = 7 id = twrbritainpolitics.452 } # conservatives attack our record
			country_event = { days = 9 id = twrbritainpolitics.458 } # conservatives make gains
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_completed_focus = ENG_go_with_freeman # went with freeman
				}
				country_event = { days = 13 id = twrbritainpolitics.454 } # freeman attacked for his youth
				country_event = { days = 15 id = twrbritainpolitics.456 } # freeman attacked for his radicalism
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { 
					has_completed_focus = ENG_go_with_gaitskell # went with gaitskell
				}
				country_event = { days = 13 id = twrbritainpolitics.455 } # butler attacked as weak
			}
			country_event = { days = 17 id = twrbritainpolitics.459 } # conservatives make gains 2
			country_event = { days = 24 id = twrbritainpolitics.460 } # minor MP scandal
			country_event = { days = 27 id = twrbritainpolitics.461 } # late stage conservative campaigning
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = lab_low_inflation_achieved
				}
				country_event = { days = 11 id = twrbritainpolitics.462 } # rewarded for low inflation
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { days = 11 id = twrbritainpolitics.464 } # punished
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = lab_low_unemployment_achieved
				}
				country_event = { days = 11 id = twrbritainpolitics.463 } # rewarded for low unemployment
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { days = 11 id = twrbritainpolitics.465 } # punished
			}
		}
	}
}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # accept it
		name = twrbritainpolitics.460.a
		add_political_power = 10
		add_to_variable = {
			var = ENG_conservative_gain
			value = 4
		}
		add_to_variable = {
			var = ENG_conservative_poll
			value = 4
			tooltip = CON_gain
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = ENG_labour_gain
				value = 4
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = ENG_labour_poll
				value = 4
			}
			set_country_flag = ENG_lab_MP_scandal
		}
	}
	option = { # try to cover it up
		name = twrbritainpolitics.460.b
		add_political_power = -35
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ENG_lab_MP_scandal
		}
		random_list = {
			50 = {
        		country_event = { days = 2 id = twrbritainpolitics.4601 }
    		}
    		50 = {
        		country_event = { days = 2 id = twrbritainpolitics.4602 }
    		}
    	}
	}
}

country_event = { #Election Results
	id = twrbritainpolitics.500
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainpolitics.500"}
	title = twrbritainpolitics.500.t
	desc = twrbritainpolitics.500.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_election

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { 
			set_country_flag = ENG_election_over
			set_country_flag = ENG_2nd_election_finished
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.500.a
		ENG_election_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					ENG = {
						check_variable = {
			                var = 1.house_of_commons_seats
			                value = ENG_COMMONS_MAJORITY
			                compare = greater_than_or_equals
			            }
					}
				}
				country_event = { days = 0 id = twrbritainpolitics.501 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					ENG = {
						check_variable = {
			                var = 3.house_of_commons_seats
			                value = ENG_COMMONS_MAJORITY
			                compare = greater_than_or_equals
			            }
					}
				}
				country_event = { days = 0 id = twrbritainpolitics.502 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { days = 0 id = twrbritainpolitics.503 }
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #2nd Election Results - labour wins
	id = twrbritainpolitics.501
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainpolitics.501"}
	title = twrbritainpolitics.501.t
	desc = twrbritainpolitics.501.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_election

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.501.a # add content
		add_political_power = 50
		#
		# the parliament mechanic stuff
		set_temp_variable =  { temp_party = 1 }
		ENG_house_of_commons_change_to_government = yes
		set_temp_variable =  { temp_party = 2 }
		ENG_house_of_commons_change_to_opposition = yes
		set_temp_variable =  { temp_party = 3 }
		ENG_house_of_commons_change_to_opposition = yes
		#
		set_country_flag = LAB_MINISTERS_ALLOWED
		set_country_flag = ENG_2ND_ELECTION_COMPLETE
		clr_country_flag = CON_MINISTERS_ALLOWED
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		# complete_national_focus = ENG_attlee_labour
		# custom_effect_tooltip = LABOUR_DECISIONS_OPENED_TT
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = LABOUR_WINS_FIRST_ELECTION # for if labour already won
				has_completed_focus = ENG_go_with_gaitskell
			}
			news_event = { days = 1 id = twrnews.245 }
			load_focus_tree = { tree = british_gaitskell_government keep_completed = yes }
			complete_national_focus = ENG_Gaitskell_government
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = LABOUR_WINS_FIRST_ELECTION # for if labour already won
				has_completed_focus = ENG_go_with_freeman
			}
			news_event = { days = 1 id = twrnews.246 }
			load_focus_tree = { tree = british_freeman_government keep_completed = yes }
			complete_national_focus = ENG_freeman_government
		}
		else = {
			news_event = { days = 1 id = twrnews.244 }
			load_focus_tree = { tree = british_wilson_government keep_completed = yes }
			complete_national_focus = ENG_wilson_minister
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Harold Wilson"
				desc = "POLITICS_WILSON_DESC"
				picture = "Harold_Wilson.dds"
				expire = "1985.1.1"
				ideology = social_democracy
				traits = {}
			}
			add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
		#Check these later - Aga
	}
}


country_event = { #2nd Election Results - conservatives win
	id = twrbritainpolitics.502
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainpolitics.502"}
	title = twrbritainpolitics.502.t
	desc = twrbritainpolitics.502.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_election

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.502.a # add content
		add_political_power = 50
		#
		# the parliament mechanic stuff
		set_temp_variable =  { temp_party = 1 }
		ENG_house_of_commons_change_to_opposition = yes
		set_temp_variable =  { temp_party = 2 }
		ENG_house_of_commons_change_to_opposition = yes
		set_temp_variable =  { temp_party = 3 }
		ENG_house_of_commons_change_to_government = yes
		#
		set_country_flag = CON_MINISTERS_ALLOWED
		set_country_flag = ENG_2ND_ELECTION_COMPLETE
		clr_country_flag = LAB_MINISTERS_ALLOWED
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = conservative
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = CONS_WIN_FIRST_ELECTION
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = ENG_magic_circles_grasp } # butler survives
			}
			news_event = { days = 1 id = twrnews.248 }
			load_focus_tree = { tree = british_focus_butler_second keep_completed = yes }
			complete_national_focus = ENG_second_butler_government
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = CONS_WIN_FIRST_ELECTION
				has_completed_focus = ENG_magic_circles_grasp # butler got removed
			}
			news_event = { days = 1 id = twrnews.249 }
			load_focus_tree = { tree = british_thorneycroft_tree keep_completed = yes } #change to thorneycroft tree
			complete_national_focus = ENG_thorneycroft_government
		}
		else = {
			news_event = { days = 1 id = twrnews.248 }
			load_focus_tree = { tree = british_focus_mac keep_completed = yes }
			complete_national_focus = ENG_macmillan_government
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Harold Macmillan"
				desc = "POLITICS_MACMILLAN_DESC"
				picture = "Harold_Macmillan.dds"
				expire = "1985.1.1"
				ideology = liberal_conservatism
				traits = {}
			}
			add_popularity = {
			ideology = conservative
			popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
		#Check these later - Aga
	}
}

country_event = { #2nd Election - con-lib coalition formed
	id = twrbritainpolitics.504
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainpolitics.504"}
	title = twrbritainpolitics.504.t
	desc = twrbritainpolitics.504.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_election

	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.504.a # add content
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = conservative
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_ideas = ENG_coalition_government_generic
		set_country_flag = ENG_2ND_ELECTION_COMPLETE
		# complete_national_focus = ENG_attlee_labour
		# custom_effect_tooltip = LABOUR_DECISIONS_OPENED_TT
		set_temp_variable =  { temp_party = 3 }
		ENG_house_of_commons_change_to_government = yes
		set_temp_variable =  { temp_party = 2 }
		ENG_house_of_commons_change_to_government = yes
		set_temp_variable =  { temp_party = 1 }
		ENG_house_of_commons_change_to_opposition = yes
		# load the normal conservative tree:
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = CONS_WIN_FIRST_ELECTION
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = ENG_magic_circles_grasp } # butler survives
			}
			load_focus_tree = { tree = british_focus_butler_second keep_completed = yes }
			complete_national_focus = ENG_second_butler_government
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = CONS_WIN_FIRST_ELECTION
				has_completed_focus = ENG_magic_circles_grasp # butler got removed
			}
			load_focus_tree = { tree = british_thorneycroft_tree keep_completed = yes } #change to thorneycroft tree
			complete_national_focus = ENG_thorneycroft_government
		}
		else = {
			load_focus_tree = { tree = british_focus_mac keep_completed = yes }
			complete_national_focus = ENG_macmillan_government
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Harold Macmillan"
				desc = "POLITICS_MACMILLAN_DESC"
				picture = "Harold_Macmillan.dds"
				expire = "1985.1.1"
				ideology = liberal_conservatism
				traits = {}
			}
		}
	}
}

	fire_only_once = yes

		name = twrbritainpolitics.102.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = commonwealth_invitations

				limit = {
					#has_global_flag = canada_refused_UK_trade_deal
					CAN = {
						has_idea = COM_commonwealth_of_nations
					}
				}
				CAN = { country_event = { id = twrbritainpolitics.103 days = 1 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					#has_global_flag = australia_refused_UK_trade_deal
					AST = {
						has_idea = COM_commonwealth_of_nations
					}
				}
				AST = { country_event = { id = twrbritainpolitics.106 days = 1 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					#has_global_flag = new_zealand_refused_UK_trade_deal
					NZL = {
						has_idea = COM_commonwealth_of_nations
					}
				}
				NZL = { country_event = { id = twrbritainpolitics.109 days = 1 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SAF = {
						has_idea = COM_commonwealth_of_nations
					}
				}
				SAF = { country_event = { id = twrbritainpolitics.112 days = 1 } }
			}
			ENG = { country_event = { id = twrbritain.200 days = 6 } }
		}
		# also a hidden event for the US to raise objections #
	}
}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainpolitics.158"}
	title = twrbritainpolitics.158.t
	desc = twrbritainpolitics.158.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # targeted tax cuts
		name = twrbritainpolitics.158.a
		add_political_power = -40
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = ENG_small_tax_cuts
			days = 500
		}
		add_stability = 0.01
		custom_effect_tooltip = COALITION_STABILITY_ADD_1
		add_to_variable = {
			var = ENG_coalition_stability_var
			value = 1
		}
		ENG_increase_coalition_stability = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				30 = {
	        		country_event = { days = 10 id = twrbritainpolitics.1381 } # SORT THIS OUT
	    		}
	    		70 = {
	    		}
	    	}
		}
	}
	option = { # insist on big tax cuts
		name = twrbritainpolitics.158.b
		add_political_power = 80
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = ENG_big_tax_cuts
			days = 500
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = COALITION_STABILITY_MINUS_2
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = ENG_coalition_stability_var
			value = 2
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ENG_decrease_coalition_stability = yes
			ENG_decrease_coalition_stability = yes
			random_list = {
				30 = {
	        		country_event = { days = 10 id = twrbritainpolitics.1381 } # SORT THIS OUT
	    		}
	    		70 = {
	    		}
	    	}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = COALITION_STABILITY_MINUS_2_IDEA_TT
	}
}

country_event = { # lab-lib coalition collapses
	id = twrbritainpolitics.174
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainpolitics.174"}
	title = twrbritainpolitics.174.t
	desc = twrbritainpolitics.174.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_parliament
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.174.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = collapses_coalition_government_tt
		add_political_power = -100
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = ENG_collapsed_coalition_government
			days = 50
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_1
			}
			remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_1
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_2
				}
				remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_3
				}
				remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_4
				}
				remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_5
				}
				remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_5
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_6
				}
				remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_7
				}
				remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_7
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_8
				}
				remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_9
				}
				remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_9
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_10
				}
				remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_10
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = ENG_coalition_government_created
		clr_country_flag = ENG_lab_lib_coalition
		clr_country_flag = ENG_con_lib_coalition
		# START THE NEW ELECTION THING # (i think i put it in below, test this)
		set_country_flag = ENG_2nd_election_lab
		activate_mission = SECOND_LABOUR_time_left
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_new_election_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			clamp_variable = {
				var = ENG_labour_poll
				min = 0
				max = ENG_COMMONS_total_seat
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = ENG_conservative_poll
				min = 0
				max = ENG_COMMONS_total_seat
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = ENG_liberal_poll
				min = 0
				max = ENG_COMMONS_total_seat
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = ENG_independent_poll
				min = 0
				max = ENG_COMMONS_total_seat
			}
			set_variable = { ENG_labour_poll = 291 }
			set_variable = { ENG_conservative_poll = 311 }
			set_variable = { ENG_liberal_poll = 20 }
			set_variable = { ENG_independent_poll = 3 }
			set_variable = { ENG_COMMONS_total_seat = 625 }
		}
	}
}

					has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_2
				}
				remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_3
				}
				remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_4
				}
				remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_5
				}
				remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_5
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_6
				}
				remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_6
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_7
				}
				remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_7
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_8
				}
				remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_8
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_9
				}
				remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_9
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ENG_coalition_stability_10
				}
				remove_ideas = ENG_coalition_stability_10
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = ENG_coalition_government_created
		clr_country_flag = ENG_lab_lib_coalition
		clr_country_flag = ENG_con_lib_coalition
		# START THE NEW ELECTION THING # (i think i put it in below, test this)
		set_country_flag = ENG_2nd_election_con
		activate_mission = SECOND_CONS_time_left
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_new_election_tt
		country_event = { id = twrbritainpolitics.400 hours = 0 }
		hidden_effect = {
			clamp_variable = {
				var = ENG_labour_poll
				min = 0
				max = ENG_COMMONS_total_seat
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = ENG_conservative_poll
				min = 0
				max = ENG_COMMONS_total_seat
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = ENG_liberal_poll
				min = 0
				max = ENG_COMMONS_total_seat
			}
			clamp_variable = {
				var = ENG_independent_poll
				min = 0
				max = ENG_COMMONS_total_seat
			}
			set_variable = { ENG_labour_poll = 311 }
			set_variable = { ENG_conservative_poll = 291 }
			set_variable = { ENG_liberal_poll = 20 }
			set_variable = { ENG_independent_poll = 3 }
			set_variable = { ENG_COMMONS_total_seat = 625 }
		}
	}

country_event = { #The New Prime Minister - Gaitskell
	id = twrbritainpolitics.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainpolitics.3"}
	title = twrbritainpolitics.3.t
	desc = twrbritainpolitics.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_parliament
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.3.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Hugh Gaitskell"
			desc = "POLITICS_GAITSKELL_DESC"
			picture = "Britain_SD_Hugh_Gaitskell.dds"
			expire = "1985.1.1"
			ideology = social_democracy
			traits = {}
		}
		news_event = { days = 1 id = twrnews.27 }
	}
}

country_event = { #The Rally
	id = twrbritainpolitics.13
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainpolitics.13"}
	title = twrbritainpolitics.13.t
	desc = twrbritainpolitics.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_parliament
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.13.a
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { mosley_opposition > 0 }
		}
		country_event = { days = 0 id = twrbritainpolitics.57 }
	}
	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.13.b
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { mosley_opposition = 0 }
		}
		country_event = { days = 0 id = twrbritainpolitics.57 }
	}
	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.13.c
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { mosley_opposition < 0 }
		}
		set_country_flag = ENG_no_mosley_coup
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { days = 10 id = twrbritainpolitics.59 }
		}
	}
}

			factor = 10

			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.16.b

			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Question of Military Spending
	id = twrbritainpolitics.23
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainpolitics.23"}
	title = twrbritainpolitics.23.t
	desc = twrbritainpolitics.23.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_parliament
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.23.a
	}

	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.23.b
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = ENG_reduced_military_spending
			days = 1000
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		add_threat = -2
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = ENG_LAB_var_inflation
			value = 0.5
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_inflation_decrease_0.5
		add_to_variable = {
			var = ENG_LAB_var_unemployment
			value = 0.2
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_unemployment_increase_0.2
		custom_effect_tooltip = MILITARY_READINESS_LOSE_10
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = ENG_defence_readiness_level
			value = 10
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Keep Rationing or nah
	id = twrbritainpolitics.29
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainpolitics.29"}
	title = twrbritainpolitics.29.t
	desc = twrbritainpolitics.29.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_rationing
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.29.a
		add_political_power = 70
		add_timed_idea = { idea = ENG_rationing_over days = 730 }
		add_to_variable = {
			var = ENG_var_moderniser_support
			value = 3
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = ENG_var_traditionalist_support
				value = 3
			}
			clamp_ENG_conservative_variables = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = MODERNISER_gain_3
		if = {
			limit = {
			    has_idea = ENG_economic_downturn
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = ENG_balance_of_payments_-0.25_tt
	        add_to_variable = {
	            var = ENG_balance_of_payments_var
	            value = -0.25
	        }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = twrbritainpolitics.29.b
		add_to_variable = {
			var = ENG_var_traditionalist_support
			value = 3
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = ENG_var_moderniser_support
				value = 3
			}
			clamp_ENG_conservative_variables = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = turn_conservatives_against_PM
		custom_effect_tooltip = TRADITIONALIST_gain_3
	}
}

country_event = { # Rail ridership falls
	id = twrbritainflavour.78
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainflavour.78"}
	title = twrbritainflavour.78.t
	desc = twrbritainflavour.78.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_railway_map
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = twrbritainflavour.78.a
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = rail_ridership_falls_UK
		}
		if = {
            limit = {
                 has_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_8
            }
            swap_ideas = {
                 remove_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_8
                 add_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_7
            }
        }
		if = {
            limit = {
                 has_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_7
            }
            swap_ideas = {
                 remove_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_7
                 add_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_6
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                 has_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_6
            }
            swap_ideas = {
                 remove_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_6
                 add_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_5
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                 has_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_5
            }
            swap_ideas = {
                 remove_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_5
                 add_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_4
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                 has_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_4
            }
            swap_ideas = {
                 remove_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_4
                 add_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_3
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                 has_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_3
            }
            swap_ideas = {
                 remove_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_3
                 add_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_2
            }
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                 has_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_2
            }
            swap_ideas = {
                 remove_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_2
                 add_idea = ENG_railway_improvements_level_1
            }
        }
	}
}

country_event = { # Calder Hall nuclear plant - delays
	id = twrbritainflavour.79
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritainflavour.79"}
	title = twrbritainflavour.79.t
	desc = twrbritainflavour.79.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_nuclear_energy
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # throw in more funding
		name = twrbritainflavour.79.a
		add_political_power = -50
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = ENG_extra_construction_costs_calder_hall
			days = 20
		}
	}
	option = { # accept the delays
		name = twrbritainflavour.79.b
		add_days_remove  = {
		    decision = calder_hall_nuclear_plant
		    days = 50
		}
	}
}

			days = 2000

country_event = { # hidden event for coalition collapse or no
	id = twrbritain.1004
	hidden = yes
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event twrbritain.1004"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_war_with = GER
						has_war_with = HSS
						has_war_with = HGR
					}
				}
				ENG = { country_event = { id = twrbritainpolitics.176 days = 1 } }
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = ENG_lab_lib_coalition
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = GER
						}
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = HSS
						}
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = HGR
						}
					}
					ENG = { country_event = { id = twrbritainpolitics.174 days = 1 } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_flag = ENG_con_lib_coalition
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = GER
						}
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = HSS
						}
						NOT = {
							has_war_with = HGR
						}
					}
					ENG = { country_event = { id = twrbritainpolitics.175 days = 1 } }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	title = twrbritain.1004.t
	desc = twrbritain.1004.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_uk_map

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = twrbritain.1004.a
	}
}
